                                    5733    1244.     *
                                    5734    1245.     *    VAMTASK INITIALIZATION ENTRY POINT
                                    5735    1246.     *
                                    5736    1247.     *        VAMTASK IS ENTERED HERE ON THE FIRST "SVC" CALL, AND DOES
                                    5737    1248.     *        ANY NECESSARY INITIALIZATION, THEN MODIFIES THE ADDRESS IN
                                    5738    1249.     *        THE VAMINFO CONTROL BLOCK TO POINT TO VAMENTER FOR
                                    5739    1250.     *        SUBSEQUENT CALLS.  THE REGISTERS ARE RESTORED AND VAMENTER
                                    5740    1251.     *        IS CALLED AS IF ENTERED DIRECTLY FROM THE USER PROGRAM.
                                    5741    1252.     *
                                    5742    1253.     ********************************************************************
